< Review>
Amazing margaritas and great burgers. We've been going to Mango's once a month for Bingo night and the food and service is always amazing, even with how packed and crazy it gets.
The mango margarita is definitely my favorite, the garlic fries are perfect.
Large beer selection. Outdoor seating. Friendly service.</Review>

<Review>Fantastic breakfast and coffee spot with really well made food. Honestly one of the best breakfasts I‚Äôve ever had.

I ordered the Traditional Breakfast with eggs over easy, sausage patty, and sourdough toast. I am super impressed with how fresh everything tasted and how well it was prepared.

The eggs were exactly as ordered and held a lot of flavor. The toast was nice and hearty with the perfect amount of butter.  Sausage patty was handcrafted and fairly lean with a really pleasant and light spiced flavor.

< Text>
Another great breakfast at a reasonable price. I love to try all the independent coffee shops we have in Long Beach and this one is a favorite. Nicolas is such a great welcoming person that is so helpful and knowledgeable about everything on the menu. The menu has a great variety for a small place. I had the traditional breakfast with the house made sausage patty, scrambled eggs and a huge,savory, homemade biscuit. My husband had the triple berry smoothie which was light and very berry! The drip coffee was good plus you get a free refill! Everything is made from scratch with the freshest ingredients plus the price is reasonable. What I paid for our whole breakfast is what I pay at other trendy coffee shops for one avocado toast and small coffee!! So if you want good, fresh, filling, homemade food, in a great ambiance, try the Steel Cup Cafe!!</Text>

< Review>
I had a lovely two night stay! I did stay during a quieter time, and I can see how it could be a little more roudy during busier times, but it was perfect for me. There are trails around the lake that you can walk to directly from the cabins and it's gorgeous. Restaurant was closed because of COVID, so I can't speak to that piece. The one CON that I do see, is paying a resort fee - with the restaurant closed, and not partaking in golf or tennis, I didn't see the point of the extra charge. Would rather have that lumped into the cost or optional if you want to use the facilities.</Review>

Very nice location that is very scenic and convenient to the lake and hiking.   Nice room, though dated.Could not sleep one night of our stay due to a large crowd of people yelling, laughing, and sledding down a hill right next to our room from 9 PM past midnight.  Front desk was unavailable to help as they leave after 8 PM. Was told only maintenance emergencies are addressed after this time.  There was no charcoal, matches, or bbq tools provided for the unclean, inconvenient, and shared, charcoal grill that was available.  A gas grill on the deck would have been nice. No dishwasher, and kitchen utensils are bare bones.</review>

< text>
We had a great time here and it was a beautiful time of year.  So just a few things I would note if your considering a stay.   One, the lake view is nice but it‚Äôs not really possible to walk from your chalet right to the lake, because the slope is so steep.   You can take a little stroll to wagon creek bridge and other parts of the lake.  It‚Äôs really nice.  As other people noted the furniture is very dated.  Kind of feels like your using your grandparents cabin, but it does give it a cozy feel.  Something more modern may appeal to younger couples but if your a little older or have a family with ya it‚Äôs probably not going to bother you at all.  If anything it may help you feel a little more comfortable.  With that said, man our bed was broken in and just needed to be replaced. So if you get chalet 143, sleep in the smaller of the two rooms.  The kitchen was well equipped but we were a little confused on where to throw away trash once it got full and there were no steak knives, which would of been nice because this place just screams steak dinner.   Lastly, the internet was surprisingly decent. I unfortunately had to do some work and was able to download some large files and hosted a few zoom meetings with no issues at all. Overall, We really enjoyed our stay and will probably be back.<//text>

< review>
I really liked that the property was nestled in the trees and backed up to Lake Siskiyou, with beautiful nature trails right out our back door.  It was very serene, and felt more remote than it was. It was well-stocked with everything we needed (except a bathtub.) We were there off-season, during the week and part of the weekend, which was good for both the quiet and our budget. It will probably be much more crowded during high season, but then again, so will all the other places in the area. I would come back here anytime.< /review>

<user_id>100843894863337905128<//user_id>< name>
Lorinda Forrest Meyer<//name>
<Date>1575818754456<//Date>< rate>
3</rate>
< review>
In the spirit of full disclosure, I have not  stayed at the resort hotel as a guest and have not yet played a round of golf. I have attended several meetings, dined there, and visited the pro shop a couple of times. As for first impressions, the building and features appear tired and a little dated, in need of freshening up. Every time I enter the lobby, I appreciate being welcomed by the front desk staff. The pro shop staff are also friendly and helpful as well. Otherwise, my experience with the restaurant and banquet staff has been luke-warm. It is as though they have lost a spark of enthusiasm in working with guests. Based on my experience as a business consultant for many years, I've found this general malaise tends to stem from something amiss in senior management. Also, the food is middle of the road. The quality is okay, in a Sysco kind of way, but lacks that memorable dining experience a resort should exude. I'm not going to speculate the underlying cause of these issues, but a place like the Mt Shasta Resort is critical on so many levels to our local community and economy. The overall guest experience should be more of a top priority than it currently appears to be. Three stars feels a bit of a harsh judgement, but I struggle with providing a four star rating because of my comments above.< /review>

Overall: it was good

Cons: Expensive!

The prices listed on Google are incorrect. They are half the prices of what they actually charge. Or maybe this place just charged me double?

My order was a burger and basket of rings/fries

Google has it listed: 7.99 + 3.99.
Ryders charged me: 13.99 + 7.99.
